        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





## Vulnerability introduction and Vulnerability lifetime



<span class="line"><!---->## Vulnerability introduction and Vulnerability lifetime<!----></span>



<br>





This vulnerability was Introduced in a performance optimization in 2021.7



<span class="line"><!---->This vulnerability was Introduced in a performance optimization in 2021.7<!----></span>



<br>





->



<span class="line"><!---->-&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





https://sqlite.org/forum/forumpost/2d76f2bcf65d256a



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://sqlite.org/forum/forumpost/2d76f2bcf65d256a"><!---->https://sqlite.org/forum/forumpost/2d76f2bcf65d256a<!----></a>



<br>





Sometimes, the inner order by in select statement is unnecessary so that SQLite will ignore it when executing this kind of query, which causes a UAF vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->Sometimes, the inner order by in select statement is unnecessary so that SQLite will ignore it when executing this kind of query, which causes a UAF vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





It affects all sqlite versions since 3.37.0.



<span class="line"><!---->It affects all sqlite versions since 3.37.0.<!----></span>



<br>





I was able to verify this vulnerability on Chrome stable, and considering this sqlite version has been out for almost a year, it may have been in Chrome for a long time, please fix it soon.



<span class="line"><!---->I was able to verify this vulnerability on Chrome stable, and considering this sqlite version has been out for almost a year, it may have been in Chrome for a long time, please fix it soon.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





## Root Cause



<span class="line"><!---->## Root Cause<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[0] When the sqlite3Select function is processing the select statement, it will traverse the pEList, pOrderBy and pHaving node on the select statement, and save all the pointers of AGG_FUNCTION and AGG_COLUMN to pAggInfo.



<span class="line"><!---->[0] When the sqlite3Select function is processing the select statement, it will traverse the pEList, pOrderBy and pHaving node on the select statement, and save all the pointers of AGG_FUNCTION and AGG_COLUMN to pAggInfo.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] After that, the sqlite3Select function will continue to generate code for the pHaving node on the select statement, and if the pHaving node is also a select statement, it will recursively call the sqlite3Select function.



<span class="line"><!---->[1] After that, the sqlite3Select function will continue to generate code for the pHaving node on the select statement, and if the pHaving node is also a select statement, it will recursively call the sqlite3Select function.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[2] For the reason of speed optimization, pOrderBy node on pHaving node may be released during processing. 



<span class="line"><!---->[2] For the reason of speed optimization, pOrderBy node on pHaving node may be released during processing. <!----></span>



<br>





This optimization was introduced in: 



<span class="line"><!---->This optimization was introduced in: <!----></span>





https://sqlite.org/forum/forumpost/2d76f2bcf65d256a



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://sqlite.org/forum/forumpost/2d76f2bcf65d256a"><!---->https://sqlite.org/forum/forumpost/2d76f2bcf65d256a<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





[3] However, the released pOrderBy node may be an AGG_FUNCTION and its pointer was previously saved in pAggInfo.This pointer will be used in the subsequent resetAccumulator function, which causes a UAF vulnerability.



<span class="line"><!---->[3] However, the released pOrderBy node may be an AGG_FUNCTION and its pointer was previously saved in pAggInfo.This pointer will be used in the subsequent resetAccumulator function, which causes a UAF vulnerability.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[0] 



<span class="line"><!---->[0] <!----></span>



<br>





```cpp



<span class="line"><!---->```cpp<!----></span>



<br>





sqlite3ExprAnalyzeAggList(&sNC, pEList);



<span class="line"><!---->sqlite3ExprAnalyzeAggList(&amp;sNC, pEList);<!----></span>



<br>





sqlite3ExprAnalyzeAggList(&sNC, sSort.pOrderBy);



<span class="line"><!---->sqlite3ExprAnalyzeAggList(&amp;sNC, sSort.pOrderBy);<!----></span>



<br>





if( pHaving ){



<span class="line"><!---->if( pHaving ){<!----></span>



<br>





  if( pGroupBy ){



<span class="line"><!---->  if( pGroupBy ){<!----></span>



<br>





    assert( pWhere==p->pWhere );



<span class="line"><!---->    assert( pWhere==p-&gt;pWhere );<!----></span>



<br>





    assert( pHaving==p->pHaving );



<span class="line"><!---->    assert( pHaving==p-&gt;pHaving );<!----></span>



<br>





    assert( pGroupBy==p->pGroupBy );



<span class="line"><!---->    assert( pGroupBy==p-&gt;pGroupBy );<!----></span>



<br>





    havingToWhere(pParse, p);



<span class="line"><!---->    havingToWhere(pParse, p);<!----></span>



<br>





    pWhere = p->pWhere;



<span class="line"><!---->    pWhere = p-&gt;pWhere;<!----></span>



<br>





  }



<span class="line"><!---->  }<!----></span>



<br>





  sqlite3ExprAnalyzeAggregates(&sNC, pHaving);



<span class="line"><!---->  sqlite3ExprAnalyzeAggregates(&amp;sNC, pHaving);<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->finalizeAggFunctions(pParse, pAggInfo); <!----></span>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->sqlite3ExprIfFalse(pParse, pHaving, addrOutputRow+1, SQLITE_JUMPIFNULL); //----&gt;[1]<!----></span>



<br>





selectInnerLoop(pParse, p, -1, &sSort,



<span class="line"><!---->selectInnerLoop(pParse, p, -1, &amp;sSort,<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->                &amp;sDistinct, pDest,<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->                addrOutputRow+1, addrSetAbort);<!----></span>

```cpp

if( pSub->pOrderBy!=0



<span class="line"><!---->if( pSub-&gt;pOrderBy!=0<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!----> &amp;&amp; (p-&gt;pOrderBy!=0 || pTabList-&gt;nSrc&gt;1)      /* Condition (5) */<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!----> &amp;&amp; OptimizationEnabled(db, SQLITE_OmitOrderBy)<!----></span>

            ("omit superfluous ORDER BY on %r FROM-clause subquery\n",i+1));



<span class="line"><!---->            ("omit superfluous ORDER BY on %r FROM-clause subquery\n",i+1));<!----></span>

  sqlite3ExprListDelete(db, pSub->pOrderBy); //---->[2]



<span class="line"><!---->  sqlite3ExprListDelete(db, pSub-&gt;pOrderBy); //----&gt;[2]<!----></span>

  pSub->pOrderBy = 0;



<span class="line"><!---->  pSub-&gt;pOrderBy = 0;<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->sqlite3VdbeResolveLabel(v, addrReset);<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->resetAccumulator(pParse, pAggInfo); //----&gt;[3]<!----></span>

```cpp

static void resetAccumulator(Parse *pParse, AggInfo *pAggInfo) {



<span class="line"><!---->static void resetAccumulator(Parse *pParse, AggInfo *pAggInfo) {<!----></span>



<br>





    //......



<span class="line"><!---->    //......<!----></span>



<br>





		for(pFunc=pAggInfo->aFunc, i=0; i<pAggInfo->nFunc; i++, pFunc++){



<span class="line"><!---->		for(pFunc=pAggInfo-&gt;aFunc, i=0; i&lt;pAggInfo-&gt;nFunc; i++, pFunc++){<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->		    if( pFunc-&gt;iDistinct&gt;=0 ){<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->			      Expr *pE = pFunc-&gt;pFExpr;<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->			      assert( ExprUseXList(pE) );<!----></span>

The zName here can be controlled to any value.



<span class="line"><!---->The zName here can be controlled to any value.<!----></span>



<br>





However, at the end of this function, a call to the sqlite3ErrorMsg function can output what zName points to.



<span class="line"><!---->However, at the end of this function, a call to the sqlite3ErrorMsg function can output what zName points to.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Therefore, this can cause a **any address read**.



<span class="line"><!---->Therefore, this can cause a **any address read**.<!----></span>

It took me a while to adapt the poc of the exploitable section in the issue description to the current stable Chrome, the version number is Version 103.0.5060.114 (Official Build) (64-bit)



<span class="line"><!---->It took me a while to adapt the poc of the exploitable section in the issue description to the current stable Chrome, the version number is Version 103.0.5060.114 (Official Build) (64-bit)<!----></span>

hi, @dcheng, @ayui, @asully



<span class="line"><!---->hi, @dcheng, @ayui, @asully<!----></span>



<br>





My fuzz found a new UAF in WebSQL.



<span class="line"><!---->My fuzz found a new UAF in WebSQL.<!----></span>



<br>





I analyzed its root cause and provided a temporary patch.



<span class="line"><!---->I analyzed its root cause and provided a temporary patch.<!----></span>



<br>





To my surprise, another vulnerability may have existed in Chrome for 7 years, and I can confirm that it was introduced in sqlite 3.9.0 in 2015.

So it is not a patch bypass for this vulnerability.

 issue

<h3 class="medium-heading"><!----> issue</h3>


          


            

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
      

<style>
        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);

           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */

        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }

          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }

          margin-bottom: 0.75em;
        }
      </style>
